 rajya ke bade meena netaa dow kirodi laal meena yaheen se aate hai or sabase dilachasp baat ye he ki wo ek baar phirabijepike saath aa gaye hai, jisase congress kii mushkilen bad sakati hai

 unhone apni rashtriya janatantric party (rajpa) kaa vilay bhi bijepi main kar diya he

 haalanki, pehle meena bijepi main hi the, lekin 2008 main unhone apni alag party bana lee thi

 jile kaa chunavi samikarnayaha kul 4 vidhansabha seat hai, jinamein se chaaron seat bijepi ke paas hai

 jile kii 2 seat saamaanya varg ke liye hai, jabaki 1-1 seat anusuchit jati (SC) or anusuchit janajati (ST) ke liye aarakshati he

 bamanwaas sidhnusuchit janajati ke liye arakshit yah seat tonk-savai madhopur loksabhaa kshetra ke antargat aati he

 Banning of possessing or using mobile phones for minor girls has been banned in a village in Mehsana district of Gujarat
 yah pratibandh is daawey ke saath lagaaya gaya he ki gajet in ladakiyon kaa dhyaan padhai se bhatkaate hai
 This ban has been imposed recently by the Panchayat of Suraj village in Kadi taluka of Mehsana
 naaballig ladakiyon ko yadi mobile paas rakhte hue yaa uskaa istemaal karte hue paaya gaya to unpar 2100 rupee kaa jurmaana lagaaya jayega
 They will have the freedom to use their parents' mobile phones only indoors
 gaanv ke sarpanch devashi wankar ke anusaar, yah faisla panchayat ne sarvasammati se liya he kyonki adhiktar graminon ko lagata he ki mobile phone ladakiyon or unke mata-pita ke liye pareshaaniyaan paidaa kar rahe hai
 The village panchayat also considered cell phones as a medium used by young lovers to run away from their homes
 wankar ne kaha, â€˜â€˜sabhi gramin un schuli ladakiyon ke mobile phone ke istemaal par pratibandh lagane ke liye sahamat ho gaye hai, jinaki umr 18 saal se kam he
 People of all communities have agreed on this, whether they are Dalits, Patels, Thakurs or Rabari
 hamane is niyam kaa ulanghan karne waalon par 2100 rupee kaa jurmaana lagaaya he
 '' wankar ne kaha, â€˜â€˜ladakiyon ko apane mata-pita ke mobile kaa istemaal apane ghar ke andar or unki dekharekh main karne kii ijaajat he
 But she cannot roam the village with a mobile
 â€™â€™ yah pratibandh sirf schuli chaatraon tak simit he or college jane vaali yuvatiyon ko panchayat ne chhot di he
 "college girls are mature enough to distinguish good and bad," said Wanker
 iske alaava, unhen apane mata-pita ke sampark main rahane ke liye mobile phone kii jarurat hoti he kyonki college hamaare gaanvon main nahin balki paas ke shaharon main hote hai
 Justifying the ban on minor girls, he said that this rule is necessary to 'protect' girls from this technique
 wankar ne kaha, â€˜â€˜sabhi jaanate hai ki aaj kii duniya main mobile phonon ke kaaran kya hota he
 This is Kali Yuga

 mahabuuba mufti or umr abdulla 35e main chhedchhad se bachane ko kah rahe hai
 In these ten points you can understand well what is ARTICLE 35A
 1
 ARTICLE 35 a was added to the Constitution in 1954, 7 years after the independence of the country
 ye anuchhed nehru cabinet kii sifarish par tatkaaleen raashtrapati dow
 Was added to the Constitution by an order of Rajendra Prasad
 2
 The only basis of ARTICLE 35A is the agreement that was signed between Prime Minister Jawaharlal Nehru in 1952 and then Prime Minister of Jammu and Kashmir Sheikh Abdullah
 ise dilli agreement bhi kehete hai
 3
 is agreement main bhartiya naagarikta ke maamle ko jammu-kashmir ke sandarbh main rajya kaa vishay mana gaya he
 Therefore, Kashmiris get some special rights in it
 isamen unke liye niyam bhi tay hai
 4
 ARTICLE 35 a main naukariyon, sampatti kii kharid-farokht, viraasat, scolership, sarkari madad or kalyankari yojanaon se judi suvidhaon ke sambandh main ye visheshadhikaar die gaye hai
 5
 ARTICLE 35 a raashtrapati ke aadesh se samvidhan main joda gaya:raashtrapati kaa ye aadesh samvidhan ke anuchhed 370 (1) (d) ke tahat jari kiya gaya tha
 This provision empowers the President to change and waive the need in the Constitution on the subject of the state in the case of Jammu and Kashmir
 6
 The special thing related to ARTICLE 35A is that while making it, it was added to the constitution by order of the President instead of the process of making laws from the parliamentary system
 jabaki samvidhan kaa anuchhed 368 (i) samvidhan main kisi bhi sanshodhan kaa adhikaar sirf sansad ko detaa he
 7
 ARTICLE 35 a se jammu-kashmir rajya kii sarkaar un logon ko sthai nivasee maanati he jo 14 may 1954 ke pehle jammu-kashmir main bas gaye the
 These residents get benefits in buying land, government jobs and government schemes in Jammu and Kashmir
 8
 ARTICLE 35 a also decides that a resident of another state cannot make a residence here as a permanent resident in Jammu and Kashmir
 ye hi nahin kisi duusare rajya ke nivasee kashmir main jameen bhi nahin kharid sakate hai
 9
 shaadi ke bare main bhi ARTICLE 35 a alag niyam nirdhaarit karata he
 According to the rules, if a woman from Jammu and Kashmir marries a person from any other state of India, then her rights are taken away, though in the case of men, these rules are different
 10
 Many years ago, a petition filed in the Supreme Court sought to abolish such discriminatory rules and implement similar laws across the country
